		numb char;
		status int;
	 	cur cursor for select "MaNLQ" from public."NguoiLienQuanCovid";
begin
    open cur;
	fetch next from cur into Ma;
	loop 
		numb := SUBSTRING ( Ma ,7 , 1 );

 			elseif (numb = '2' or numb = '3' or numb = '9') then status := 1;
